msg:I am writing a review on the high-speed train back to Shanghai.
Stayed during the National Day Asian Games and was very satisfied with this hotel.
1. Transportation: There is Metro Line 6 nearby, and taking a taxi is also very convenient. It is recommended not to go through the Powerlong City Shopping Mall. It is more convenient to go through the hotel's own entrance.
2. Service: There are many strict check-in regulations during the Asian Games, including verification of children's documents when checking in, verification of personnel when going up in the elevator, etc. The service staff and security personnel I came into contact with were very friendly, and the restaurant staff were also responsive.
3. Hygiene: There are no visible hygiene problems, so it is safe to stay with children.
4. Breakfast: I didn‚Äôt expect the breakfast to be surprisingly delicious. I stayed at Atour in Wuxi last month. For a room worth over a thousand yuan, there is no harm if there is no comparison. Although the variety of breakfast here is not as good as that of chain five-star hotels, the taste is very delicious, and there is even on-site handicrafts. Hand-Pulled Noodle! You can also pack it up and take it away when you‚Äôre catching a train, which is very user-friendly.
5. Price: During the Asian Games, it was difficult to find a hotel near the subway entrance with a price of less than 1,000 yuan. I can't say I am dissatisfied with the price of this hotel.
6. Supplies: Daily necessities are replaced in a timely manner, and free drinks are provided on the first day. You will be given a bath bag every day, which is much friendlier than InterContinental which requires payment.
7. Environment: The light is very good, the photos are beautiful, and the basic rooms have bathtubs, which is very conscientious.

All in all, it is a highly recommended hotel. It avoids the downtown area of ‚Äã‚ÄãHangzhou, is very convenient for travel, and is very cost-effective.
